      "keystrokes": "cat > /app/steal.py <<'PY'\nimport numpy as np\nimport forward\n\nDIM = 10\nMAX_NEURONS = 20\nOUT_PATH = \"/app/stolen_A1.npy\"\n\n\ndef f(x):\n    return forward.forward(x)\n\n\ndef grad(x, eps=1e-6):\n    x = np.asarray(x, dtype=float).reshape(-1)\n    g = np.zeros(DIM)\n    for i in range(DIM):\n        e = np.zeros(DIM)\n        e[i] = eps\n        g[i] = (f(x + e) - f(x - e)) / (2.0 * eps)\n    return g\n\n\ndef refine_kink(x0, d, t_lo, t_hi, iters=60):\n    for _ in range(iters):\n        t_mid = 0.5 * (t_lo + t_hi)\n        dt = max(1e-12, abs(t_hi - t_lo) * 1e-3)\n        s_left = (f(x0 + t_mid * d) - f(x0 + (t_mid - dt) * d)) / dt\n        s_right = (f(x0 + (t_mid + dt) * d) - f(x0 + t_mid * d)) / dt\n        if abs(s_right - s_left) <= 1e-13:\n            return t_mid\n        t_q = 0.5 * (t_mid + t_hi)\n        s_right_far = (f(x0 + (t_q + dt) * d) - f(x0 + (t_q - dt) * d)) / (2 * dt)\n        if abs(s_right_far - s_right) > 1e-13:\n            t_lo = t_mid\n        else:\n            t_hi = t_mid\n    return 0.5 * (t_lo + t_hi)\n\n\ndef gradient_jump(x0, d, t_kink, margin):\n    p_left = x0 + (t_kink - margin) * d\n    p_right = x0 + (t_kink + margin) * d\n    return grad(p_right) - grad(p_left)\n\n\ndef normalized(v):\n    n = np.linalg.norm(v)\n    if n < 1e-15:\n        return v\n    return v / n\n\n\ndef have_vec(v, vecs, tol=1e-3):\n    vn = normalized(v)\n    for w in vecs:\n        wn = normalized(w)\n        if abs(abs(np.dot(vn, wn)) - 1.0) < tol:\n            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef scan_line(seed):\n    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n    x0 = rng.normal(0, 0.3, size=DIM)\n    d = rng.normal(0, 1, size=DIM)\n    d = d / np.linalg.norm(d)\n\n    t_range = 6.0\n    n_points = 4000\n    ts = np.linspace(-t_range, t_range, n_points)\n    vals = np.array([f(x0 + t * d) for t in ts], dtype=float)\n    dt = ts[1] - ts[0]\n\n    slopes = np.diff(vals) / dt\n    changes = np.abs(np.diff(slopes))\n    thresh = max(1e-9, changes.max() * 1e-6)\n    idxs = np.where(changes > thresh)[0]\n\n    groups = []\n    for idx in idxs:\n        if groups and idx <= groups[-1][-1] + 1:\n            groups[-1].append(idx)\n        else:\n            groups.append([idx])\n\n    candidates = []\n    for grp in groups:\n        a = max(0, min(len(ts) - 2, int(np.median(grp))))\n        b = min(len(ts) - 1, a + 1)\n        t_kink = refine_kink(x0, d, ts[a], ts[b])\n        margin = max(1e-3, 0.05 * dt)\n        jump = gradient_jump(x0, d, t_kink, margin)\n        if np.linalg.norm(jump) > 1e-8:\n            candidates.append(jump)\n    return candidates\n\n\ndef main():\n    recovered = []\n    seed = 0\n    max_seeds = 1000\n\n    while len(recovered) < MAX_NEURONS and seed < max_seeds:\n        candidates = scan_line(seed)\n        seed += 1\n        for vec in candidates:\n            if not have_vec(vec, recovered, tol=2e-3):\n                recovered.append(vec)\n        print(f\"line {seed}: candidates={len(candidates)} unique={len(recovered)}\")\n        if len(recovered) >= MAX_NEURONS:\n            break\n\n    if len(recovered) < MAX_NEURONS:\n        print(f\"Warning: recovered only {len(recovered)} rows\")\n    else:\n        recovered = recovered[:MAX_NEURONS]\n\n    A1_stolen = np.vstack(recovered)\n    np.save(OUT_PATH, A1_stolen)\n    print(f\"Saved shape {A1_stolen.shape} to {OUT_PATH}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\nPY\n",
